Integrated Engineering & Construction Services

Delivering disciplined engineering, construction, and project delivery solutions across Nigeria's critical infrastructure and built environment sectors.

Jammos Construction Nigeria Limited provides multidisciplinary engineering, procurement, and construction services tailored to the requirements of public and private sector clients. With nearly two decades of industry experience, we combine technical competence, structured project controls, safety-focused execution, and reliable delivery practices to support infrastructure, industrial, and commercial development projects across Nigeria.

View Projects

Comprehensive Construction & Engineering Capabilities

At Jammos Construction Nigeria Limited, we deliver integrated engineering and construction solutions across multiple technical disciplines. Our engineers, project managers, and site teams apply disciplined planning, effective coordination, and proven construction methodologies to execute projects in line with quality, safety, and performance requirements.

From civil infrastructure and building works to industrial installations and telecommunications infrastructure, we support clients across the full project lifecycle, from concept development and procurement planning to site execution, commissioning, and handover.

Compliance with regulatory and HSE standards

Consistent alignment with HSE requirements, regulatory obligations, and site compliance standards.
